<p><b>штам<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-штамп-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штаны́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štaný</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штано́в</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a> (2621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Staat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">state, country</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">stāt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">staet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">stātus</i>. The semantic development was influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">état</i> from the same Latin source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štat</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>шта́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>state <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a political division, e.g. a US state</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>staff <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">personnel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штат.html>штат</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>staff, personnel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расписание.html>расписа́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnoje</b> raspisánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff list; manning table; salary schedule</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>staff
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> prepodavátelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff teacher/professor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> rabótnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">staff member</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>standard, regular, normal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:режим.html>режи́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnyj</b> režím</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standard/nominal/normal mode</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>routine, nonemergency
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:штатный.html>шта́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>štátnaja</b> situácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">normal/routine situation; non-emergency</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***штольня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штольня.html>што́льня</a> (29938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sztolnia</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">stolnia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stollen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gallery, adit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">stolle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gallery, adit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b>што́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>пать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:заштопать.html>зашто́пать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-штоп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штора.html>што́ра</a> (5879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Strafe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">punishment, penalty, fine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štraf</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штра́фа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штра́фы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штра́фов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fine, penalty, citation</li>
<li>Soviet army penal battalion of World War II.</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štraf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штрафной.html>штрафно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štrafnój</span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> penalty</li>

***штука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a> (1647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sztuka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, in turn from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stück</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">shtick</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>piece, each (in counting items)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свеча.html>свеча́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одна́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svečá — odná <b>štúka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Candle — one each (= one candle)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što éto za <b>štúka</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What sort of <b>thing</b> is this?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ка</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot tak <b>štúka</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a mess!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thousand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:штука.html>шту́ку</a></b> ба́ксов <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On mne <b>štúku</b> báksov dólžen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He owes me a thousand bucks.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">aviation</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Stuka <i>(German Junkers Ju 87 dive bomber)</i></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">štukatúrka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штукатурка.html>штукату́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stucco, plaster</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloqial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ironical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heavy make-up, slap</li></ol>
